NOTICE
NO LEGAL RESPONSIBILITY IS ACCEPTED FOR THE PUBLICATION OF ADVERTISEMENTS REGARDING
CHANGE OF NAME IN THE TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE. PERSONS NOTIFYING THE CHANGES
WILL REMAIN SOLELY RESPONSIBLE FOR THE LEGAL CONSEQUENCES AND ALSO FOR ANY OTHER
MISREPRESENTATION, ETC.
(By Order)

Director of Stationery and Printing.

PUBLIC NOTICES
This Public Notice is issued under Section 72 of the Partnership Act, on behalf of my clients
M/s. Laso Pharmaceuticals, at No.27, Ramasamy Pilai Street, Kamalakshipuram, Vellore.
This is to inform the General Public that pursuant to the Resolution passed in the Partners Meeting held on
18-7-2014, that R.Vimaladhithan, son of Ramakrishnan, aged 26 years, residing at No.145, Soolai Sabapathy Nagar,
Palavansathu Village, Vellore, has been expelled from the Partnership Firm M/s. Laso Pharmaceuticals, having Firm No.6
of 2014 (Registrar of Firms Vellore), with effect from 18-7-2014.
The general public is put to notice, not to deal with said R. Vimaladhithan, regarding any matters relating to the
Partnership Firm M/s. Laso Pharmaceuticals and if any does so, they are doing at their own risk and the neither the
continuing Partners namely M. Kavitha, S. Shoba, R. Karthik, M. Ramesh Babu, S. Kumaraswamy, D. Suresh nor the above
Partnership Firm shall be held responsible or accountable for the said acts.
6-C, Lakshmi Bhawan,
609, Anna Salai,
Chennai-600 006.
12th August 2014.

KAVITHA ASHOK,
Advocate.

BURANESWARY (Female) 48 years born on 9-3-1966, who is congenitally blind, mentally retarded, unmarried
and totally dependent daughter of K.S. Sethuraman, residing at Room No.5, Shanthi Nivas, Sri Poorna Mahameru Trust,
Subam Nagar, Old Pallavaram, Chennai-600 117, shall henceforth be known as S. BHUVANESWARI.
Chennai,
13th August 2014.

K.S. SETHURAMAN,
(Father.)
